<item>
  <title><![CDATA[Industries for HPs RPOS]]></title>
  <link>https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/14/industries-for-hps-rpos/</link>
  <pubDate>Wed, 14 Feb 2018 13:56:01 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>kayimpex</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/?p=413</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/13/introduction-to-hps-rpos/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Continued...</a>

In our <a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/13/introduction-to-hps-rpos/">previous article</a> you learnt the meaning of RPOS and what it does. In <a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/14/industries-for-hps-rpos/">this post</a> you will learn about the different industries in which the RPOS device can be used and in what way.

HPs RPOS is helpful in many industries like:
<ul>
	<li><strong>Food &amp; Beverage (F&amp;B) Industry</strong></li>
	<li><strong>Hospitality Industry</strong></li>
	<li><strong>General Merchandise Industry</strong></li>
	<li><strong>Convenience Stores</strong></li>
	<li><strong>Grocery Industry</strong></li>
</ul>
<strong></strong><!--more-->

<strong>Food &amp; Beverage Industry. </strong>

It includes the restaurants, bars, clubs, pubs, lounges, and such place where food and beverage is served. In this industry the front end operations (stewards) should coordinate with the back end operations (Kitchen staff) quickly, as it cannot be slow. And if this coordination is not there the business will not run effectively and there will be a big chaos in the restaurant. As everyone knows, in a restaurant a lot of supplies are to be used, so inventory is to be managed accurately so that they know how much stock is available and the stock should not go waste.

Here are a few points which explain where HPs RPOS can be used in the Food &amp; Beverage (F&amp;B) industry. There are many different <a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/13/introduction-to-hps-rpos/">HPs RPOS</a> devices which can be used in the Food &amp; Beverage industry.
<ol>
	<li>HPs Digital Signage can be put up in restaurants on which they can show their promotions of the restaurant or any new dish that they have come up with or any discounts/offers going on the restaurants.</li>
	<li>By using HP ElitePad mobile POS Solution, restaurants can lessen the communication gap between the stewards and the kitchen staff. The orders taken by the stewards can be directly sent to the kitchen staff instead of walking to the kitchen and giving the written order.</li>
	<li>HP RP7 Retail System is IP54 certified, which mean that it is water and dust resistant. The fanless unit stops water and dust from entering the device. This is very useful in the kitchen and service areas.</li>
	<li>Customer Facing Display (CFD) is the display screen which is shown to the customers which can help in additional advertising and promotions. It can also display what order have you placed and what is the subtotal of your order. Such devices can be seen at McDonalds.</li>
	<li>The HPs RP5 Retail System helps tracking the integration between restaurants, supply chains and operations. This helps to reduce the out of stock instances which can ensure smooth movement in the industry from stocking up the materials to out of stock products, it keeps track of everything. But for this the Sales Reporting and Inventory Tracking Software has to be installed in it.</li>
	<li>HPs RP5 Retail System helps in tracking your workforce management and performances which helps in perfect distribution of workforce and employee efficiency. But for this you will have to install the Workforce Management Software.</li>
</ol>
&nbsp;

&nbsp;

[caption id="attachment_419" align="aligncenter" width="1024"]<img class=" size-large wp-image-419 aligncenter" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/02/hotel-1_2.jpg?w=1024" alt="hotel-1_2" width="1024" height="683" /> POS Device at a Restaurant[/caption]

<strong></strong>

<strong>Hospitality Industry</strong>

Hospitality industry includes hotels; lodging, and entertainment business, customers are becoming demanding for a better experience where they stay. It is very important for a business to provide its customers with better service keeping the budget in mind and controlling the cost and focus on satisfying their customers with their best services and benefits to their regular customers.

Here are a few points which explain where HPs RPOS can be used in the Hospitality Industry. There are different <a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/13/introduction-to-hps-rpos/">HPs RPOS</a> devices which can be used in the Hospitality Industry.
<ol>
	<li>HPs Digital Signage can be put up at the reception for visitors to have a look at whats new in the hotel, what offers are going on, any travelling offers, city sights seeing, famous places in the respective city, etc.</li>
	<li>HPs RP7 Retail system comes with a 10 display, its Customer Facing Display (CFD) which helps the customer to verify the billing details while making the payment. It can also help in promotion of the hotel.</li>
	<li>HPs ElitePad POS solution helps the customers to access additional services comfortably sitting in their hotel room. With the help of HPs ElitePad POS Solution the customer can order food, call for room service with just a touch of a finger.</li>
	<li>HP Retail System helps the Hospitality Industry right from the front desk to back office which improves business efficiencies.</li>
	<li>HPs Retail System helps the hotel to track the purchase preference of the guests and give them some reward points for their benefit.</li>
</ol>
&nbsp;

&nbsp;

<strong>General Merchandise Industry </strong>

In the General Merchandise Industry the more the customer waits at the store, his size of the shopping basket will increase more. For keeping continued sales you need a strong supply chain management with real time sales and inventory data.

Here are a few points which explain where <a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/13/introduction-to-hps-rpos/">HPs RPOS</a> can be used in the General Merchandise Industry. There are different HPs RPOS devices which can be used in the General Merchandise Industry.
<ol>
	<li>HPs Digital Signage Display can be displayed in the store front i.e. on the display near the entrance or behind the billing counter. HPs Digital Signage helps bring in customers in the store and it also helps in promotions.</li>
	<li>HPs ElitePad Mobile POS has a Magnetic Stripe Reader (MSR), Barcode Scanner which helps the merchant to stay by the side of the customer and not leave the customer. The sales person can stay by the side of the customer and give information about a product which is in the inventory to the customer by using the HPs ElitePad Mobile POS Solution. With the HPs ElitePad Mobile POS the sales person can do the complete transaction including the billing without leaving the customers side.</li>
	<li>HPs RP7 All-in-One Retail system gives high speed services. It is available as a wall mounted device or a table top device. The HPs RP7 All-in-One Retail device is apace saving which has got ports on all sides to connect the Magnetic Stripe Reader (MSR), Finger Print Reader, webcam or scanner which is needed. All the peripherals are sold separately.</li>
	<li>HPs RP5 Retail System helps you to manage you workforce/manpower which is put up in the store, this includes all parts of the store. For this you will have to install the Workforce Management Software in the HPs RP5 Retail System device.</li>
	<li>HPs Retail System helps the store to operate the front end and the back end of the store to improve business efficiency.</li>
</ol>
<strong></strong>

<strong>Convenience Store Industry</strong>

Convenience Store such as those found in gas stations or chain stores such as 7-elevens, Big Bazars, etc. which offer their customers a wide range of products.

Here are a few points which explain where HPs RPOS can be used in the Convenience Store Industry. There are different <a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/13/introduction-to-hps-rpos/">HPs RPOS</a> devices which can be used in the Convenience Store Industry.
<ol>
	<li>HPs digital Signage Display can portray attractive and engaging in-store displays to show the promotions of the store. This results in the customer to stay longer in the store and also result in increase of sales of the store.</li>
	<li>HPs ElitePad Mobile POS Solution is a very adaptive device. It can be used as a self service kiosk for customers to use for information on any product or getting to know about any promotion. The HPs ElitePad Mobile POS can be used by the staff of the store to handle the stock which comes additional with a bar code scanner.</li>
	<li>HPOs Retail System which is touch enabled, flexible, high performance and do not cause any problem for anyone. This helps the store handlers to checkout as many customers as possible which help in not waiting in long queues. This will make the customer happy and the customer experience will be more pleasant.</li>
	<li>HPs Retail System helps you to manage store outlets, supply chain and operational departments. With the use of HPs Retail System the business can reduce out of stock good or over stocked good. For all this you will have to install the Sales Reporting and Inventory Tracking Software.</li>
	<li>HPs Retail System combined with HPs POS application can track the loyal customers and the store can award them with reward points for their loyalty. The system involves a loyalty program which tracks the customers.</li>
</ol>
&nbsp;

<strong>Grocery Industry </strong>

Grocery Store and Supermarkets have a large amount of customers and more than that a large amount of products on daily basis. It is very important for them to maintain a good communication between the store, supply chain and operations to make sure that that distribution or products and inventory is done in a systematic manner. Particularly on weekends the amount of customers are very high. It is very important for the checkout process to be productive and reliable.

Here are a few points which explain where HPs RPOS can be used in the Grocery Industry. There are different HPs RPOS devices which can be used in the Grocery Industry.
<ol>
	<li>HPs Digital Signage can be put up in these stores or supermarkets to serve the customers. It can also be put up as a self service kiosk where customers can access to know about store promotions, or if they want information about any product in the store.</li>
	<li>HPs ElitePad Mobile Solution POS device that includes an Magnetic Stripe Reader, Bar Code Scanner, which helps the store person to go around the store and help the customer if they are facing any problem while they are in the store. The sales person can also do the billing of the customer on the HPs ElitePad Mobile POS to reduce the long queues at the billing counter.</li>
	<li>HPs RP5 Retail System gives a good performance to handle high amount of transactions in supermarkets. The advanced processors and advanced technologies help in supporting the demanding retail applications, large installation and point of sale multi tasking.</li>
	<li>HPs Retail System helps you to manage store outlets, supply chain and operational departments. With the use of HPs Retail System the business can reduce out of stock good or over stocked good. For all this you will have to install the Sales Reporting and Inventory Tracking Software.</li>
	<li>HPs Retail System combined with <a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/13/introduction-to-hps-rpos/">HPs POS</a> application can track the loyal customers and the store can award them with reward points for their loyalty. The system involves a loyalty program which tracks the customers.</li>
</ol>
&nbsp;

[caption id="attachment_423" align="aligncenter" width="600"]<img class=" size-full wp-image-423 aligncenter" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/02/bigstock-woman-with-groceries-waiting-i-76845098small.jpg" alt="Woman with groceries waiting in line at the supermarket checkout" width="600" height="400" /> RPOS Device at a Grocery Store[/caption]

&nbsp;

In the <a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/16/hps-rpos-products/">next article</a> you will learn about the different RPOS products used by different industries and in what way are they used, so stay tuned.

<item>
  <title><![CDATA[HPs RPOS Products]]></title>
  <link>https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/16/hps-rpos-products/</link>
  <pubDate>Fri, 16 Feb 2018 11:14:18 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>kayimpex</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/?p=435</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/14/industries-for-hps-rpos/">Continued...</a>

<strong>Retail Point Of Sale</strong>abbreviated as<strong>RPOS</strong>. It is that device which is used in the retail selling of any product. It is used where an invoice is made at the end of any purchase. But it is not only that, when a customer walks into a store he not only comes to buy things and just leave. He expects the retailer to understand him and engage with him. RPOS can help the retailer serve the customer in a flexible manner to improve in-store connections. It can also help retailers to provide seamless and consistent brand experience.<!--more-->

<a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/13/introduction-to-hps-rpos/">HPs RPOS</a> is more sophisticated than a cash register<span id="more-380"></span>or PC. Including a keyboard with magnetic stripe reader, receipt printer, customer display pole, or touchscsreen monitor, and a wide selection of software applications.

In our <a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/14/industries-for-hps-rpos/">previous post</a>, we explained all the <a href="https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/02/14/industries-for-hps-rpos/">Industries </a>where the RPOS products will be useful and of what will the be useful for.

&nbsp;

[caption id="attachment_384" align="aligncenter" width="1024"]<img class="alignnone size-large wp-image-384" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/02/rp3000-bigger.jpg?w=1024" alt="Rp3000-bigger" width="1024" height="955" /> RPOS System[/caption]

&nbsp;

The products which are included in the RPOS(Retail Point of Sale) are given below:
<ol>
	<li>HP ElitePad Mobile POS</li>
	<li>HP RP7 Retail System</li>
	<li>HP RP5 Retail System</li>
	<li>HP RP3 Retail System</li>
	<li>HPs Digital Signage Solutions</li>
</ol>
&nbsp;

<strong>1. HPs ElitePad Mobile POS Solution</strong>

The HPs ElitePad Mobile POS Solution has a great design, build to last longer, works right from the front end to the back end of the store. The HPs Retail Jacket which is like a cover to the HPs ElitePad Mobile POS Solution, which comes with a built in Magnetic Stripe Reader (MSR) and Barcode Scanner. Both HPs ElitePad Mobile POS Solution and HPs Retail Jacket if combined together allows the store person to speed up the checkout process of the customers so that they dont have to wait in the long queues for making the bill payment. This will also result in increase the sales of the store and the store people can attend more customers. Which will in turn result in more customers to come in the store as the service is fast. The HPs ElitePad Mobile POS Solution can also help you in managing the workforce in the store, inventory management, which will take the store experience to another level.

[caption id="attachment_461" align="aligncenter" width="1024"]<img class="alignnone size-large wp-image-461" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/02/5f0a79a0734b227ebc52a33dbe05212bbd98cc8d_gallery.jpg?w=1024" alt="5F0A79A0734B227EBC52A33DBE05212BBD98CC8D_gallery" width="1024" height="854" /> HP ElitePad Mobile POS[/caption]

Interacting with the customers in the store using the mobile sales tool on the HPs ElitePad Mobile POS Solution. The sales person on the store floor can do the complete transaction of a customer using the HPs Retail Jacket which has a built in MSR(Magnetic Stripe Reader) and barcode scanner.

On HPs Retail Jacket the hand strap in the back give the store person to hold the device perfectly in palm without any discomfort and awkward slips.

[caption id="attachment_462" align="aligncenter" width="550"]<img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-462" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/02/retailjacket_gallery_image2_tcm_195_1596758.jpg" alt="HP ElitePad Mobile POS Solution, Catalog, Back" width="550" height="460" /> HP ElitePad Jacket[/caption]

The HPs Retail Jacket has a secondary battery which keeps you working for a longer time without any charging interruption.

The HPs ElitePad Mobile POS Solution has been designed to resist vibration, high and low temperatures, dust, shock, drop and humidity.

&nbsp;

<strong>2. HPs RP7 Retail System</strong>

The HPs RP7 Retail System is a sleek and modern design which fits into the retail and hospitality environments. The HPs RP7 Retail System is a space saving device which is customised to fulfil your stores unique and ever changing requirement.

The HPs RP7 Retail System is a flush bezel edges make this an appealing self service kiosk that compliments any modern retail environment.

[caption id="attachment_467" align="aligncenter" width="1006"]<img class="alignnone size-large wp-image-467" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/02/img_20996277_high_1493324500_5588_20202.jpg?w=1006" alt="img_20996277_high_1493324500_5588_20202" width="1006" height="1024" /> HP RP7 Retail System[/caption]

The HPs RP7 Retail System can be used on the billing counter or it can also be wall mounted for better operation.

The HPs RP7 Retail System is compatible with a full range of retail products such as MSR, Barcode Reader, fingerprint scanner webcam, which can be connected to the HPs RP7 Retail System. All the additional products are to be brought separately.

To know more about The HPs RP7 Retail System search for HP RP7 on YouTube.

&nbsp;

<strong>3. HP RP5 Retail System</strong>

The HP RP5 Retail System has a lot of advanced features that helps the retailers to adapt to one system which does everything like critical operations, the expandable and highly configurable HP RP5 Retail Systems allows business to customise a complete solution that is specifically designed for use in the retail stores.

The HP RP5 Retail System is available with Intel processors, mass storage, removable media and memory.

[caption id="attachment_471" align="aligncenter" width="1024"]<img class="alignnone size-large wp-image-471" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/02/img_31573280_high_1493228765_0482_31719.jpg?w=1024" alt="img_31573280_high_1493228765_0482_31719" width="1024" height="380" /> HP RP5 Retail System Front[/caption]

The HP RP5 Retail System, just like HPs RP7 Retail System, connects with other compatible devices such as MSR, Barcode Scanner, Fingerprint Reader, webcam, etc.

The HP RP5 Retail System is made very reliable, retail hardened engineering helps reduce the computer to go out of service and which will increase the use of it.

[caption id="attachment_480" align="aligncenter" width="1024"]<img class="alignnone size-large wp-image-480" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/02/rp5_retail_system_gallery_image_2_tcm183_2260943_tcm183_2109415_tcm183-2260943.jpg?w=1024" alt="RP5_Retail_System_gallery_image_2_tcm183_2260943_tcm183_2109415_tcm183-2260943" width="1024" height="494" /> HP RP5 Retail System Back[/caption]

To know more about The HPs RP5 Retail System search for HP RP5 on YouTube.

<strong></strong>

<strong>4. HP RP3 Retail System</strong>

The HP RP3 Retail System is affordable and compact which provides the retailers a good connectivity feature that helps to increase operating cost efficiency. The space constrained settings are nearly everywhere, where you need a POS system. The HP RP3 Retail System can set up as a traditional client or a thin computing platform which is put all over the stores wherever needed.

[caption id="attachment_476" align="aligncenter" width="1024"]<img class="alignnone size-large wp-image-476" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/02/c03484384_1750x1285.jpg?w=1024" alt="c03484384_1750x1285" width="1024" height="752" /> HP RP3 Retail System[/caption]

The compact design of the HP RP3 Retail System frees up the counter space and can be set up anywhere, where a POS is required.

The HP RP3 Retail System has been shock tested and the extreme environmental conditions can withstand any rough use towards the system.

The HP RP3 Retail System reduces energy costs with ENERGY STAR qualified and EPEAT Gold registered design.

To know more about The HPs RP3 Retail System search for HP RP3 on YouTube.

&nbsp;

<strong>5. HPs Digital Signage Solutions </strong>

HPs Digital Signage Solutions which are put up displays advertisements which reach the key audience which helps to grow revenue, of the respective industry, which will make your communications more relevant and memorable. HPs Digital Signage Display, combined with the HPs Digital Signage Player is designed to deliver dynamic and interactive signage content that attracts, engages, and promotes effectively to customers.
<ul>
	<li>HPs Digital Signage Display</li>
</ul>
HPs Digital Signage Display reaches to the customers with expansive, high-resolution video, graphics, and texts with vibrant colours and deep rich tones.

HPs Digital Signage Display is built to last for a longer time and it can run 24/7. HP offers a 3 year limited warranty backed by HP service and support.

[caption id="attachment_484" align="aligncenter" width="1024"]<img class="alignnone size-large wp-image-484" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/02/a982653c1b6c2af0aad9fd899901f80f16ab9b91_gallery.jpg?w=1024" alt="A982653C1B6C2AF0AAD9FD899901F80F16AB9B91_gallery" width="1024" height="651" /> HP Digital Signage Display[/caption]

HPs Digital Signage Display is fully tested, qualified for out of the box functionality, and it is also compatible with HP business products for a seamless solution.
<ul>
	<li>HPs Digital Signage Players</li>
</ul>
HPs Digital Signage Players have high contrast ratios, brightness and the flexible positioning for stunning views of graphics and text.

HPs Digital Signage Players features the latest graphics configuration, latest processors and chips with very high graphics, the power you need to run a compelling digital signage content.

[caption id="attachment_489" align="aligncenter" width="1024"]<img class="alignnone size-large wp-image-489" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/02/b1b2c9d8-491f-4a09-9dac-95bc7cab4350-e1518773911382.jpg?w=1024" alt="B1B2C9D8-491F-4A09-9DAC-95BC7CAB4350" width="1024" height="376" /> HP Digital Signage Player[/caption]

HPs Digital Signage Players are pre certified by Independent Software Vendors (ISVs) and is backed by HPs 3 year onsite warranty for years of smooth and reliable performance.

&nbsp;

<item>
  <title><![CDATA[Artificial Intelligence can now Debate with a Human.]]></title>
  <link>https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/06/25/artificial-intelligence-can-now-debate-with-a-human/</link>
  <pubDate>Mon, 25 Jun 2018 12:54:07 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>kayimpex</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/?p=556</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<p style="text-align:center;"><strong>Project Debater an Artificial Intelligence can now debate with humans.</strong></p>
<img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-558" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/projectdebater_social.jpg?w=1024" alt="ProjectDebater_Social" width="1024" height="536" />

Think about it, we are talking about an AI that can take on expert human debaters by responding to arguments using unscripted reasoning to persuade an audience to consider its position on a controversial topic. <strong>IBMs Project Debater</strong> is a language-reasoning AI system that is built to facilitate intelligent debate.

<!--more-->

<strong>What is Project Debater?</strong>

A system that brings AI to the art of debate. Project Debater is the first AI system that can debate humans on complex topics. Project Debater digests massive texts, constructs a well-structured speech on a given topic, delivers it with clarity and purpose, and rebuts its opponent. Eventually, Project Debater will help people reason by providing compelling, evidence-based arguments and limiting the influence of emotion, bias, or ambiguity.

&nbsp;

<strong>Goal</strong>

The goal of the project is to challenge narratives that have become one-sided in our society. The team says that the capabilities of such an AI can help uncover hard facts that challenge the rise of misinformed and distorted views.

In a demonstration, IBMs Project Debater argued, delivered rebuttals and summaries against the worlds top debaters. Both sides were given four minutes to deliver an opening statement, followed by a four minute rebuttal and a two minute summary. The topics ranged from subsidising space exploration to telemedicine and debater convincingly argued on each.

What makes this even more interesting is that none of them had previous knowledge of the topics presented to them. The entire debate was unscripted and unrehearsed.

&nbsp;

Project Debater moves us a big step closer to one of the great boundaries in AI: mastering language. It is the latest in a long line of major AI innovations at IBM, which also include Deep Blue, the IBM system that took on chess world champion Garry Kasparov in 1997, and IBM Watson, which beat the top human champions on Jeopardy in 2011.

The new technology will build on the solid foundation, IBMs AI that beat human players on the televised show Jeopardy! Project Debater will expand the capabilities of API from which it borrows its Speech to Text capabilities from. Debater will contribute advanced language and dialogue features.

&nbsp;

<strong>What makes Project Debater Unique?</strong>

Building the system was a remarkably difficult and complex challenge. Over the past six years, a global IBM Research team endowed Project Debater with three capabilities, each breaking new ground in AI:
<ol>
	<li>Data-driven speech writing and delivery.</li>
	<li>Listening comprehension that can identify key claims hidden within long continuous spoken language.</li>
	<li>Modelling human dilemmas in a unique knowledge graph to enable principled arguments, wrote the company in a blog post.</li>
</ol>
&nbsp;

<strong>Testing</strong>

The Project Debater was put to tests on the 18<sup>th</sup> of June 2018 at an event in San Francisco. The AI went head-to-head on two topics: whether space exploration should be subsidized, and whether we should increase the use of telemedicine.

In both debates, the audience voted Project Debater to be worse at delivery but better in terms of knowledge. And despite several robotic slip-ups, the audience voted the AI to be more persuasive in terms of changing the audience's position than its human opponent, in the second debate.

The competition followed a traditional debate format: Project Debater and its human challenger each presented a four-minute opening speech, then a four-minute rebuttal, and a two-minute closing statement. The system mines hundreds of millions of articles from numerous well-known newspapers and magazines searching for the most relevant points to support or contest the topic at hand.

The debate topic is not known in advance, and Project Debater is not pre-trained on any specific topic claims IBM.

&nbsp;

<strong>Aim</strong>

IBM now aims to demonstrate it's possible for humans to have meaningful discussions with a machine. The goal is to build a system that helps people make evidence-based decisions when the answers aren't black-and-white. In the future, we believe machines will be able to help humans with many important decisions we make daily.

<img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-557" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/adobestock_138972731.jpeg?w=1024" alt="AdobeStock_138972731" width="1024" height="632" />

Project Debater, which has been in the works since 2012, can automatically generate a whole speech, reminiscent of an opinion article, and deliver it persuasively. The system then uses Watson Speech to Text to listen to the human debater's side and prepare its rebuttal. IBM says Project Debater can listen to and unpack up to four minutes of continuous spoken speech.

Because it is a machine, Project Debater is impartialit isn't out to prove a position or to be right. It is designed to help expand minds and help people see more than one side of an issue.

&nbsp;

<strong>When can I see Project Debater in action?</strong>

The Project Debater will soon be in action. Watch this Space for further updates.

&nbsp;

Email us your enquiries: <a href="mailto:sales@kayimpex.com">sales@kayimpex.com</a>

<item>
  <title><![CDATA[HP Device as a Service (DaaS)]]></title>
  <link>https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/07/04/hp-device-as-a-service-daas/</link>
  <pubDate>Wed, 04 Jul 2018 09:05:59 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>kayimpex</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/?p=560</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<img class=" size-large wp-image-561 aligncenter" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/07/hp-device-as-a-service.png?w=1024" alt="HP Device As a service" width="1024" height="536" />

<strong>Smart, simplified computing solutions for your business in todays world.</strong>

<!--more-->

<strong>Introduction</strong>

HP DaaS will make your company more efficient, it will help in the Improvement of Employee Experience and it will lay off the burden from the shoulders of IT Experts.

HP DaaS will also boost employee productivity &amp; IT Efficiency with the next level of computing solutions. You will get everything you need and nothing you dont, right from hardware devices to the smallest of accessories to life cycle support &amp; services, with a specific price per device.

&nbsp;

Getting your personal device at your workplace has challenged the IT Experts in maintaining a secured IT environment. Multiple Operating Systems have opened up the endpoints for security breach, which in-turn made it difficult for the IT Experts to get the status of the IT environment.

HP DaaS simplifies these challenges by managing a diverse assortment of desktops, workstations, and mobile devices which will help in closing those unsecured end points and securing the business with HP DaaS.

&nbsp;

&nbsp;
<h2><strong>ALL ABOUT DAAS</strong></h2>
&nbsp;

<strong>The right device for the job.</strong>

<img class=" size-large wp-image-562 aligncenter" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/07/daas2.jpg?w=1024" alt="daas2" width="1024" height="576" />

There are employees in an organisation who need custom set devices as per their needs, for example, in the accounts department; the accounts department needs custom set configuration, different software, and things like latest devices.

HP DaaS provides global support accidental damage protection, next day repair/replacement services, so the employees can work on their device without stopping their work for a longer time.

&nbsp;

<strong>Manage with Insights.</strong>

<img class=" size-large wp-image-563 aligncenter" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/07/digital-enterprise-analytics-solutions.jpg?w=1024" alt="digital-enterprise-analytics-solutions" width="1024" height="576" />

HP DaaS gives you real time analytics, insights, which will help in managing and optimizing assets and resources which will in-turn help the business to grow and move forward.

HPs multi OS device management capabilities help your business in the management capabilities across all HP DaaS devices. One can also implement proactive corrective actions before your operations are affected. With the help of HP DaaS Insights HP Service Agents can monitor and diagnose the status of your devices in real time and can make the necessary changes which are required. The insights can help your business to be reliable, consistent computing experience.

Custom make your plans with additional lifecycle services, from assessment and deployment to end of use.

&nbsp;

<strong>Flexibility for your business.</strong>

<img class=" size-full wp-image-564 aligncenter" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/07/business-systems.jpg" alt="Business-Systems" width="500" height="347" />

With the help of HP DaaS you do not pay for more than what you use. You can choose from a specific list and custom make you plan. You can adjust your plan and flex down your fleet to meet the changing workforce or workload. Add lifecycle services and refresh devices as needed with the simplicity of a single contract and price per device.

With HP DaaS, you will get,
<ul>
	<li>Multi-type, multi-OS device management.</li>
	<li>Technical support and next business day service.</li>
	<li>Lifecycle management on global scale.</li>
	<li>Unique analytics.</li>
	<li>Proactive management capabilities.</li>
	<li>Flexible plans.</li>
	<li>One Stop price per device model.</li>
</ul>
<strong></strong>

<strong>One stop solution.</strong>

HP DaaS delivers world class devices and accessories that are right for the job. HP DaaS combines it with one-stop hardware support, services, fleet management which will remove a lot of work load from the shoulders of IT experts with the simplified, predictable pricing model.

<strong></strong>

<strong>End to End Life Cycle Services:</strong>

Our full portfolio of service options covers every phase of the device lifecyclefrom start to finishfor HP devices and other brands. Our expert consultants will help you choose a program to optimize your technology investment.

The steps of end to end life cycle services are:
<ul>
	<li><strong>Dispose/ Design:</strong> Create your ideal tech environment with our assessment, design, and planning services.</li>
	<li><strong>Configure:</strong> Save time and increase productivity by having your custom images and settings installed.</li>
	<li><strong>Deploy:</strong> Hit the ground running with deployment services including installation and data migration.</li>
	<li><strong>Optimize:</strong> Get the most out of your IT environment through helpdesk services, priority support, and staff augmentation.</li>
	<li><strong>Maintain:</strong> Relieve your IT staff of maintenance hassles by letting HP handle onsite service, accidental damage protection, and more.</li>
	<li><strong>Dispose:</strong> Keep your technology fresh by letting HP securely and responsibly manage hardware thats at the end of its lifecycle.</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

&nbsp;

&nbsp;

<strong>CUSTOM THE PLAN TO YOUR NEEDS</strong>

<img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-565" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/07/5ws05gka-e1530694373170.jpg" alt="5wS05gkA" width="1024" height="390" />
<ul>
	<li>Additional lifecycle services to deliver end-to-end solutions</li>
	<li>DaaS plans include options from HP Financial Services (HPFS) with 1, 2, 3, 4, or 5 year terms.</li>
	<li>Fleet Flexibility options available to flex down to match workloads available for 2, 3, 4 and 5 year terms.</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

<item>
  <title><![CDATA[The Future of Emails: I]]></title>
  <link>https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/07/10/the-future-of-emails-i/</link>
  <pubDate>Tue, 10 Jul 2018 10:00:04 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>kayimpex</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/?p=567</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[Email is the primary form of communication in any business for more than 20 years. Yet study after study proves that it lacks productivity-wasting time. On an average, an employee sends and receives 122 emails per day. They also have approximately 150 unread mails in their inbox. And the employees spend a shocking one-third time on their mail at their workplace.<!--more-->

<img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-568" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/07/email-security-spam.png" alt="email-security-spam" width="975" height="488" />

Many of the employees have a disorganised inbox which clutters the brain of employees, getting to Inbox Zero is considered as a badge of honour. At that time there were more and more companies that use AI bots like Slack, which many believed would be the final nail in emails coffin back in 2014 when Slack got popular.

Despite all the reports, feedback and response there was a point where email started growing at a very fast rate. By 2016 there were 2.6 billion email users worldwide, which have been reported to increase to 2.9 billion by 2019. Which according to statistics mean, one-third of the global population will have an email.

&nbsp;

There are many smart minds out there that are looking forward to the future of email, heres how:

<strong>Email is getting more and more secured.</strong>

<img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-569 alignleft" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/07/0_0_480_1_70__features_istock-486272596.jpg" alt="0_0_480_1_70__Features_iStock-486272596" width="480" height="360" />
<p style="text-align:left;">Recently Slack made an update in their privacy policy which lets the employers read direct message of employees without them knowing about it. So think again before you gossip about your boss if you are using Slack. Keeping gossips aside, there are more important and sensitive data which cannot be shared with people outside your organisation for which a secured email client like ProtonMail are designed for. The messages sent via ProtonMail are encrypted end to end, as the companys servers are in Switzerland, as the privacy law over there are very strict. Your business can set it up so that even admins cant access all the accounts. No team chat client can do that yet.</p>
<strong></strong>

<strong>When emails start looking and working like browsers &amp; apps</strong>

Recently Google announced a Gmail developer preview of AMP for Email. With the help of Accelerated Mobile Pages (AMP) mobile web pages load faster which they are using it to build a self-contained web experience for email. For example, you get an email from a tech company showcasing a laptop on sale, so you will get an option of directly purchasing it, without getting redirected to another page, but purchasing it directly from your inbox itself. This feature is not much of a use for internal mails or B2B mails, but this can be useful for B2C businesses where an organisation directly deals with end customers.

&nbsp;

<strong>Want emails to organise your life?</strong>

One must be getting many mails in a day, so an inbox is just like a dumping ground of many things going on around you. Just like those no-rely addresses emails you receive every day. Letting an AI scrape your mails to put meetings on your calendar is just the tip of the iceberg. Smart email client like Newton, Edison and Astro have built-in Artificial Intelligence (AI) which can filter your mail box; keeping the important mails on top, unsubscribe to spam mails and create timelines around themes like emails about an upcoming presentation or an upcoming business trip.

&nbsp;

So as of now dont bid adieu to your emails, it has a lot more to come, keeping in mind what the latest trends are in 2018.

&nbsp;

<item>
  <title><![CDATA[Edge Computing Is Changing The Network]]></title>
  <link>https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2018/07/17/edge-computing-is-changing-the-network/</link>
  <pubDate>Tue, 17 Jul 2018 11:48:38 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>kayimpex</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/?p=571</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[&nbsp;

<img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-577" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/07/edge-computing1.png" alt="edge-computing" width="802" height="240" />

Edge computing is a way to streamline the flow of traffic from IoT devices and provide real-time local data analysis

The data produced by the Internet of Things (IoT) devices is now processed closer to where it is created than sending it through longer routes to data centers or to the cloud.

By doing this the computing closer to the edge of the network lets your business analyse important data<!--more--> in real time, which is a need for organisations across many industries like Healthcare, manufacturing, telecommunication, finance, logistics and many more.

There have been many presumptions that everything will be in the cloud with a strong and stable pipe between the cloud and edge computing which is not realistic.

&nbsp;

<strong>What is edge computing?</strong>

Edge computing is a mesh network of micro data centers that process or store confidential data locally and push all received data to a central data center or cloud storage repository, in an area of less than 100 square feet.

<img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-573" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/07/egde_computing.jpg" alt="Egde_computing" width="895" height="524" />

It is referred to in IoT use cases, where edge devices would collect a huge amount of data and send it all to a data center or cloud for processing. Edge computing sorts the data locally so some of it is processed locally, reducing the backhaul traffic to the central repository.

This is usually done by the IoT devices transferring the data to a local device that includes compute, storage and network connectivity in a small form factor. Data is processed at the edge and all or a portion of it is sent to the central processing or storage repository in a corporate data center, co-location facility or IaaS cloud.

&nbsp;

<strong>Why does edge computing matter?</strong>

Edge computing deployments are ideal in a variety of circumstances. One is when IoT devices have poor connectivity and its not efficient for IoT devices to be constantly connected to a central cloud.

Other use cases have to do with latency-sensitive processing of information. Edge computing reduces latency because data does not have to traverse over a network to a data center or cloud for processing. This is ideal for situations where latencies of milliseconds can be untenable, such as in financial services or manufacturing.

Heres an example of an edge computing deployment: An oil rig in the ocean that has thousands of sensors producing large amounts of data, most of which could be inconsequential; perhaps it is data that confirms systems are working properly.

That data doesnt necessarily need to be sent over a network as soon as its produced, so instead the local edge computing system compiles the data and sends daily reports to a central data center or cloud for long-term storage. By only sending important data over the network, the edge computing system reduces the data traversing the network.

Another use case for edge computing has been the build-out of next-generation 5G cellular networks by telecommunication companies. IDC, who studied edge computing, predicts that as telecom providers build 5G into their wireless networks they will increasingly add micro-data centers that are either integrated into or located adjacent to 5G towers. Business customers would be able to own or rent space in these micro-data centers to do edge computing and then have direct access to a gateway into the telecom providers broader network, which could connect to a public IaaS cloud provider.

&nbsp;

<strong>Edge vs. Fog computing</strong>

As the edge computing market takes shape, theres an important term related to edge that is catching on: <strong>fog computing</strong>.

<img class=" size-large wp-image-574 aligncenter" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/07/fog-vs-edge-overview.png?w=1024" alt="fog-vs-edge-overview" width="1024" height="535" />

Fog refers to the network connections between edge devices and the cloud. Edge, on the other hand, refers more specifically to the computational processes being done close to the edge devices. So, fog includes edge computing, but fog would also incorporate the network needed to get processed data to its final destination.

Many organisations &amp; educational institutions are developing reference architectures for fog and edge computing deployments.

Some have predicted that edge computing could displace the cloud. Edge and fog computing are useful when real-time analysis of field data is required.

&nbsp;

<strong>Edge computing vs. cloud computing</strong>

For industrial companies to fully realize the value of the massive amounts of data being generated by machines, edge computing and cloud computing must work together.

When you consider these two technologies, think about the way you use your two hands. You will use one or both depending on action required. Apply that to an Industrial IoT example, where one hand is edge and the other hand is cloud, and you can quickly see how in certain workloads your edge hand will play a more prominent role while in other situations your cloud hand will take a lead position. And there will be times when both hands are needed in equal measure.

<img class=" size-large wp-image-572 aligncenter" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/07/edge-computing-vs-cloud-computing.jpg?w=1024" alt="Edge Computing vs Cloud Computing" width="1024" height="576" />

Scenarios in which edge will dominate include a need for low latency (speed is of the essence) or where there are bandwidth constraints (locations such as a mine or an offshore oil platform that make it neither practical nor affordable, and in some cases impossible, to send all data from machines to the cloud). It will also be important when Internet or cellular connections are spotty. Cloud computing will take a more dominant position when actions require significant computing power, managing data volumes from across plants, asset health monitoring and machine learning, and so on.

The bottom line is this: cloud and edge computing are both necessary to industrial operations to gain the most value from todays sophisticated, varied, and volume of data applied across cloud and edge, wherever it makes the most sense to achieve the desired outcomes.

&nbsp;

<strong>Edge computing security</strong>

<img class=" size-large wp-image-575 aligncenter" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/07/cyber-security-blog-min.jpg?w=1024" alt="cyber-security-blog-min" width="1024" height="569" />

There are two sides of the edge computing security.
<ul>
	<li>Some argue that security is theoretically better in an edge computing environment because data is not traveling over a network, and its staying closer to where it was created. The less data in a corporate data center or cloud environment, the less data there is to be vulnerable if one of those environments is comprised.</li>
</ul>
The other side of that is, some believe edge computing is inherently less secure because the edge devices themselves can be more vulnerable. In designing any edge or fog computing deployment, therefore, security must be a paramount. Data encryption, access control and use of virtual private network tunnelling are important elements in protecting edge computing systems.

&nbsp;

  <title><![CDATA[Azure Cloud]]></title>

  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<strong>What is Cloud?</strong>

Cloud computing is an information technology (IT) paradigm that enables ubiquitous access to shared pools of configurable system resources and higher-level services that can be rapidly provisioned with minimal management effort, often over the Internet. Cloud computing relies on sharing of resources to achieve coherence and economies of scale, similar to a public utility.<!--more-->

<img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-581" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/08/enterprise-blog-2-min.jpg?w=1024" alt="Enterprise-Blog-2-min" width="1024" height="683" />

Third-party clouds enable organizations to focus on their core businesses instead of expending resources on computer infrastructure and maintenance. Advocates note that cloud computing allows companies to avoid or minimize up-front IT infrastructure costs. Proponents also claim that cloud computing allows enterprises to get their applications up and running faster, with improved manageability and less maintenance, and that it enables IT teams to more rapidly adjust resources to meet fluctuating and unpredictable demand. Cloud providers typically use a "pay-as-you-go" model, which can lead to unexpected operating expenses if administrators are not familiarized with cloud-pricing models.

&nbsp;

<strong>What are the types of Cloud?</strong>
<ol>
	<li>Public</li>
	<li>Private</li>
	<li>Hybrid</li>
</ol>
&nbsp;

<strong>Introduction to Azure</strong>

&nbsp;

<img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-582" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/08/azure_logo.png" alt="Azure_Logo" width="461" height="130" />

&nbsp;

Microsoft Azure, formerly known as Windows Azure, is Microsoft's public cloud computing platform. It provides a range of cloud services, including those for compute, analytics, storage and networking. Users can pick and choose from these services to develop and scale new applications, or run existing applications, in the public cloud.

And those which unchecked are those services which you will have to be handled by you or your IT Manager.

&nbsp;

<strong>Why to consider cloud?</strong>
<ol>
	<li>Speed to deliver new services.</li>
	<li>Scale from 30,000 to 250,000 site visitors instantly.</li>
	<li>The on-premises service will cost approximately $100,000</li>
</ol>
&nbsp;

<strong>Azure Import/Export Service</strong>

<strong>Fast, secured, large data migration to the cloud.</strong>

Transferring large volumes of data over a network can take days, weeks or even months. Avoid the hassle and ship your physical disks directly to Azurewe will upload them for you. Take advantage of the Azure Import/Export service for Azure Storage and accelerate your cloud transition.

<strong></strong>

<strong>Why Azure Import/Export?</strong>

<strong>Efficiently migrate large data sets</strong>

Save time and money, compared to network transfer, by shipping physical disks to and from Azure. Import large amounts of initial workload data to Azure or quickly send data to your customer sites for simple content distribution. Create backups of your on-premises data to store in the cloud and then recover data to your on-premises location if needed.

<strong>Keep data private</strong>

When using the Import/Export service, your data is highly-secured every step of the way. Disks are encrypted using Microsoft BitLocker drive encryption and your encryption keys are managed on the Azure portal or Azure REST API over SSL. In the Datacenter, we migrate your data from drive to cloud using a fast, private network upload link.

<strong>Ensure data integrity</strong>

Use the Import/Export service to migrate your data with confidence. Built-in checksums and an MD5 hash ensure data integrity. Track and monitor the status of your data migration through logs and audit trails on the Azure portal.

<img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-583" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2018/08/could.jpg?w=1024" alt="cloud computing network conception" width="1024" height="576" />

<strong>What are the benefits of cloud computing?</strong>

<strong>Cost:</strong> It eliminates the cloud capital expense.

<strong>Speed:</strong> Since cloud computing services are self-services and on demand on few mouse clicks, it provides a lot of flexibility and takes the pressure off capacity planning.

<strong>Global Scale:</strong> It has the ability to scale elastically from the right geographic location.

<strong>Productivity:</strong> The IT team gets more time for important business goals.

<strong>Performance:</strong> It can scale up-down &amp; in-out on the fly as per the requirement

<strong>Reliability:</strong> Cloud computing makes data backup, DR and business continuity easier and less expensive.

&nbsp;

<strong>Traditional Data Center VS Cloud Computing</strong>

<strong>Azure can act as:</strong>
<ol>
	<li>Servers</li>
	<li>Disaster Recovery</li>
	<li>Backup Solution</li>
	<li>Website Platform</li>
	<li>Development &amp; Testing</li>
	<li>Storage</li>
</ol>
&nbsp;

<strong>Why migrate to Azure Cloud?</strong>

Azure is the only hybrid cloud to help you with cost-effective, flexible cloud migration paths. Get all the tools and resources you need to migrate your apps, data, and infrastructure at your own pace, with confidence.

<strong>Assess</strong>

Start your Azure migration by discovering and assessing your on-premises apps, data, and infrastructure. Map dependencies across applications and decide their priority for cloud migration.

<strong>Migrate</strong>

Move your apps, data, and infrastructure confidently using powerful, free tools that guide you through and automate the cloud migration journey while minimizing downtime.

<strong>Optimize</strong>

In Azure, streamline your cloud resources continuously to enhance security, improve performance, and maximize ROI with free cost management tools.

  <title><![CDATA[HP Device as a Service Steps Explained in Detailed.]]></title>
  <link>https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2019/01/29/hp-device-as-a-service-steps-explained-in-detailed/</link>
  <pubDate>Tue, 29 Jan 2019 13:27:52 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>kayimpex</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/?p=586</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[HP DaaS will make your company more efficient, it will help in the Improvement of Employee Experience and it will lay off the burden from the shoulders of IT Experts.

HP DaaS will also boost employee productivity &amp; IT Efficiency with the next level of computing solutions. You will get everything you need and nothing you dont, right from hardware devices to the smallest of accessories to life cycle support &amp; services, with a specific price per device.

<!--more-->

<strong>The landscape is changing.</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Changing Expectation</li>
	<li>Everything as a Service</li>
	<li>HP Managed Print Services</li>
	<li>Device as a Service</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

<strong>IT is not getting any easier.</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Aging Fleet</li>
	<li>Budget Pressure</li>
	<li>Business Volatility</li>
	<li>Security</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

<strong>DaaS: Reinventing how technology works for you.</strong>

Workplace transformation begins with HP DaaS, which enhances, improves, and optimizes the way your organization acquires, manages and uses technologywhile giving IT a strategic role.

<img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-587" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2019/01/daas-e1548766488500.png?w=1024" alt="daas" width="1024" height="499" />

&nbsp;

<em><strong>HP Device as a Service  Reinventing how technology works for you.</strong></em>

<strong>Enhance - Device Acquisition:</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Capex to Opex.</li>
	<li>Award winning innovative technology on regular refresh cycle.</li>
	<li>Improve cash flow and achieve predictable TCO.</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

<strong>Improve - Device Management:</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Full suite of device management lifecycle services, customized to your needs.</li>
	<li>Consistent experience across the globe.</li>
	<li>Reduce costs and free up internal IT resources, while improving end-user support.</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

<strong>Optimize - Device Usage</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Productive, secure, always-ready devices from day one to end-of-life.</li>
	<li>Active monitoring with proactive and predictive services.</li>
	<li>Fleet reporting, analytics and insights.</li>
	<li>Continual device optimization.</li>
	<li>Drive tangible business impact.</li>
</ul>
<strong> la carte solution offered in a single contract on a per-seat, per-month basis.</strong>

<strong></strong>

<strong>Above as explained below:</strong>

<strong>ENHANCE DEVICE ACQUISITION:</strong> Reinventing how technology works for you.

Give users innovative technology, built-in security, and a regular refresh cycle. Discover a new model for acquiring technology that improves cash flow and helps you achieve predictable ownership costs.

<strong>Strategically trusted</strong>: Leverage HPs expertise and scale, and bring greater value to your business.

<strong>End-of-life safe</strong>: Get ahead of technology with a solution that plans ahead for end-of-life.

<strong>Financial intelligence</strong>: Manage your total cost of ownership with contractual precision.

&nbsp;

<strong>Building your HP DaaS solution</strong>

We add to your contract your selected excellent computing devices and accessories.

Full range of HP commercial products: PCs, Thin Clients, RPOS, Workstations, Mobile Devices and accessories.

<img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-590" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2019/01/untitled2-e1548766568549.png?w=1024" alt="untitled2" width="1024" height="264" />

<strong>IMPROVE DEVICE MANAGEMENT:</strong> Reinventing how technology works for you.

Lifecycle services from configuration to device refresh improve end-user support and reduce costs, while freeing up internal IT resources. Benefit from HPs global consistency, expertise, and single point of accountability.

<strong>Satisfaction driven:</strong> Close Service gaps and deliver HP calibre service across the device lifecycle.

<strong>Monitored for security: </strong>Keep your devices monitored, secured and policy complaint at all times.

<strong>Global consistency:</strong> Have a global provider and a single point of accountability.

&nbsp;

Steps in improving device management  DaaS Services
<ol>
	<li><strong>Discovery &amp; Design </strong></li>
	<li><strong>Configuration</strong></li>
	<li><strong>Deploy</strong></li>
	<li><strong>Optimize</strong></li>
	<li><strong>Maintain</strong></li>
	<li><strong>Dispose &amp; Refresh</strong></li>
</ol>
<strong></strong>
<ol>
	<li><strong>Discover &amp; Design</strong></li>
</ol>
<img class="alignnone size-large wp-image-588" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2019/01/untitled-e1548766169272.png?w=1024" alt="untitled" width="1024" height="505" />

Understand the customers current state and objectives and design a solution.

Assessment, Discovery, Design future state personalization, solution designing and project planning are the things to remember when discovering and designing.

<strong>Benefits:</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Clarify what is working or not working in the current environment about efficiencies, helpdesk, security concerns, policies and guidelines.</li>
	<li>Assess and find the gaps by applying industry best practices.</li>
	<li>Design the services to cover the lifecycle with the best total cost of ownership and return on investment.</li>
</ul>
<strong></strong>

&nbsp;
<ol start="2">
	<li><strong>Configuration</strong></li>
</ol>
<img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-589" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2019/01/untitled1-e1548766631193.png?w=1024" alt="untitled1" width="1024" height="472" />

Devices configured according to customer requirements that will integrate into their end-user environment.

Image &amp; application, custom system settings, integration and packaging, labelling, tagging, and win 10 application transformation are the things to keep in mind when configuration is going on.

<strong>Benefits:</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Ready-to-use integrated hardware products set up according to customer IT organization and security standards.</li>
	<li>Build and customize fleet with the right image, application and settings.</li>
	<li>Installation and integration of third party hardware parts into devices.</li>
	<li>Improve device security and asset management to prevent lost or stolen assets.</li>
	<li>Global reach and consistency</li>
	<li>Cost optimization</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

&nbsp;
<ol start="3">
	<li><strong>Deploy</strong></li>
</ol>
<img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-591" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2019/01/untitled3-e1548766682533.png?w=1024" alt="untitled3" width="1024" height="440" />

Special services to deliver secure and deploy devices that fits your organizations requirements.

PC Deployment project management, logistics, installation and setup, migration, and executive services.

<strong>Benefits:</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Streamline operational processes through a consistent installation of devices.</li>
	<li>Reduce in-house labour cost and focus IT resources on value-added tasks.</li>
	<li>Minimize downtime through fast, professional, and expert deployment of devices.</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

&nbsp;
<ol start="4">
	<li><strong>Optimize</strong></li>
</ol>
<img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-592" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2019/01/untitled4-e1548766726524.png?w=1024" alt="untitled4" width="1024" height="430" />

Services to help with end-user readiness.

Helpdesk, moves, adds and changes, priority services, proactive intelligence, data, and device security are the things to remember when optimizing DaaS.

<strong>Benefits:</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Maximize productivity of end-user</li>
	<li>Improve specific requirements for security and manageability.</li>
	<li>Fast troubleshooting of devices/reduce downtime.</li>
	<li>Get reports about IT performance.</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

&nbsp;
<ol start="5">
	<li><strong>Maintain</strong></li>
</ol>
<img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-593" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2019/01/untitled5-e1548766785754.png?w=1024" alt="untitled5" width="1024" height="547" />

Easy access to repair services for optimal uptime.

On-site services, resident engineers, multi-vendor, accidental damage protection, defective medical retention are the points to keep in mind when maintaining a DaaS.

<strong>Benefits:</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Minimize impact of downtime and increase performance of existing processes.</li>
	<li>Focus IT resources on value-added tasks.</li>
	<li>Reduce IT costs/budget.</li>
	<li>Reduce security breach impact.</li>
	<li>Manage sensitive data effectively</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

&nbsp;
<ol start="6">
	<li><strong>Dispose &amp; Refresh</strong></li>
</ol>
<img class=" size-large wp-image-594 aligncenter" src="https://kayimpex.files.wordpress.com/2019/01/untitled6-e1548766824881.png?w=1024" alt="untitled6" width="1024" height="412" />

Safely and securely decommission and refresh end-of-life devices.

Data wipe, recycling or disposal, device refresh are the things to be kept in mind while disposing.

<strong>Benefits:</strong>

Refresh of hardware/dispose of old hardware.

Decrease a large stock of old hardware.

Wiping data from retired hardwaresecurely and worry-free.

Recycling of hardware in compliance with applicable legislative practices and environmental regulations.

&nbsp;

&nbsp;

<strong>OPTIMIZE DEVICE USAGE: </strong>Reinventing how technology works for you

Delight your users and transform your workplace with productive, secure, always-ready devices. Monitor devices with Proactive Intelligence*analytics that anticipate problems, and optimize fleet performance and productivity. You can see a tangible impact on your business.

<strong>Lifecycle productivity:</strong> Make users happy with devices that are well tuned and productive.

<strong>Dashboard insights:</strong> Gain analytical insight on your fleets inventory, location, and condition.

<strong>True customization:</strong> Let HP manage all your devices with an ideal service mix.

<strong>Workplace optimization:</strong> Get proactive support and issue resolution through Proactive Intelligence and Tech Caf.

&nbsp;

<strong>Management and analytics</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Global single point of contact</li>
	<li>Customer advocate inside HP</li>
	<li>Part of the HP account team</li>
	<li>Service performance reporting</li>
	<li>Hardware performance reporting</li>
	<li>Manages any issues and escalations</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

<strong>WHY HP DAAS?</strong>

<strong>Service and ecosystem to deliver DaaS:</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Devices</li>
	<li>Services</li>
	<li>Management and Analytics</li>
</ul>
<strong>Commercial agreement:</strong>
<ul>
	<li>As a Service- Choose your service, define your team. Single contract per seat per month.</li>
	<li>Flexibility to meet customers needs- Inside Service Contract, Outright Purchase, Direct Lease, and Capex to Opex.</li>
</ul>
<strong>The HP difference:</strong>
<ul>
	<li>Monitoring, managing, reporting and analytics</li>
	<li>End point device management expertise</li>
	<li>Print &amp; Personal Systems</li>
	<li>Multiple Payment Options</li>
	<li>Direct &amp; Channel Enablement</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

<strong>Summary</strong>
<ul>
	<li>HP can supply your PC and Print Services across their complete lifecycle around the globe with one contract and fixed monthly payments.</li>
	<li>HP has the highest Recommend rating of the top PC OEMs.</li>
	<li>Consider the many other cost-saving and improved experience services from HP.</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

Request a more detailed discussion with a Services Sales Specialist.

<item>
  <title><![CDATA[HP DaaS Proactive Management (HP DPM) - Service Definition - Part 1]]></title>
  <link>https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/2019/02/19/hp-daas-proactive-management-hp-dpm-service-definition-part-1/</link>
  <pubDate>Tue, 19 Feb 2019 07:54:05 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>kayimpex</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://kayimpex.wordpress.com/?p=597</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<ol>
	<li><strong>SERVICE OVERVIEW</strong></li>
</ol>
HP Device as a Service (DaaS) is a modern service model that simplifies how organizations equip their employees with the right hardware, support, and lifecycle services. Our goal is to improve end user productivity and security while providing customers and IT with performance, agility, and cost predictability.

As part of HP DaaS, Proactive Management with HP TechPulse provides multi-OS device management services, comprehensive insights, and reports for the device fleet. HP offers three plans: Standard, Enhanced, and Premium. Standard is designed for customers who want to manage and secure their own endpoints but want to leverage the unique insights and reports from HP TechPulse to do this more effectively and with greater visibility to issues that are impacting end-user productivity. Enhanced and Premium packages include multi-OS device management and security policy enforcement by specialized HP Service Experts. HP Service Experts are trained and certified in unified, multi-OS endpoint management technology and will assist IT in delivering proactive security, support, and device management. Please note that Proactive Management does not include any form of onsite break-fix support or any onsite support Service Level Agreement (SLA), however, these can be purchased separately and included in the HP DaaS contract.<!--more-->

HP TechPulse is the HP analytics and machine learning platform that provides rich insights at the fleet level while also providing detailed insights and recommendations at the individual device/user level. HP TechPulse uses machine learning, preconfigured logic, and contextual data to deliver device, application, and usage insights which help customers optimize IT spending, resources and perhaps most importantly, end user productivity and security. Customers can view dashboards of their environment and reports for all enrolled devices, including non-HP devices1. The HP DaaS Proactive Management and TechPulse platform is cloud-based and offers flexibility and scalability for customers who have mobile users and multiple device and OS types at multiple locations. HP TechPulse analytics and reporting gives customers that single pane of glass, holistic view of their multi-OS fleet through an intuitive dashboard.

&nbsp;

&nbsp;

<strong></strong>
<ol start="2">
	<li><strong>PREREQUISITES</strong></li>
</ol>
HP Proactive Management service has dependencies on systems, network, and some important customer information.

<strong>System Requirements:</strong>

DaaS Proactive Management with HP TechPulse:
<ul>
	<li>Windows 7.0 SP1</li>
	<li>Windows 8.1</li>
	<li>Windows 10</li>
	<li>Android v4.4 and up</li>
	<li>iOS 10.0 and up9</li>
	<li>MacOS 10.12 and up</li>
</ul>
Browser requirements for HP DaaS portal. Windows PC web browsers:
<ul>
	<li>Google Chrome for Windows: Version 68.0 or higher</li>
	<li>Internet Explorer for Windows: Version 11 or higher (Windows 7 SP1 or 8.1 only)</li>
	<li>Firefox for Windows: Version 61.0 or higher</li>
	<li>Microsoft Edge for Windows: 40.0 or higher</li>
	<li>Mobile OS browsers</li>
	<li>Chrome on Android: 68 or higher</li>
	<li>Safari on iOS 10 or higher</li>
	<li>Safari on MacOS 10.12 or higher</li>
</ul>
Supported HP Retail Point of Sale (RPOS) systems. HP DaaS Proactive Management analytics client support for HP retail point of sale (RPOS) devices. Retail Point of Sale Devices:
<ul>
	<li>HP RP9 G1 Model 9015, 9018, 9115, 9118</li>
	<li>HP MP9 G4</li>
	<li>HP RP5 Model 5810</li>
	<li>HP Engage One (includes former ElitePOS Model 141,143,145)</li>
	<li>HP Engage Flex Pro</li>
	<li>HP Engage Flex Pro-C</li>
	<li>HP Engage Go</li>
</ul>
<strong>Network requirements:</strong>

An Internet connection is required for communications between the managed devices and the HP cloud management service.

<strong>Prerequisites for Onboarding:</strong>

Onboarding is the process of transitioning all customer devices covered under the DaaS plan into HP Proactive Management using the HP TechPulse solution. The following information and activities are required to proceed with the on-boarding project. The responsibility to provide the required information to the Onboarding Program Manager falls to the customer, the HP Account Manager, and/or the reseller/partner:
<ul>
	<li>Customer primary contact (name, email, phone, and location information). NOTE: This should be the IT contact for the customer or partner who will be working with HP to deploy the software agent to the devices.</li>
	<li>Customer company address</li>
	<li>(Enhanced and Premium Plan) Customer device list to be managed by HP Proactive Management. Device model and serial number are needed when we enrol the devices into Workspace ONE. A template will be provided during the on-boarding process.</li>
	<li>Customer User Principal Name (UPN) (Example: bob.smith@mycompanyname123.com )</li>
	<li>Active Directory DNS domain name (for example: hp.com)</li>
	<li>Customer list of report admins</li>
	<li>Implemented firewall and proxy settings</li>
	<li>Install and run the Proactive Management network assessment tool.</li>
</ul>
<strong></strong>

<strong></strong>
<ol start="3">
	<li><strong>ROLES AND RESPONSIBILITIES:</strong></li>
</ol>
<strong>Primary Service roles and personas:</strong>

Depending on the HP DaaS Proactive Management plan and options purchased, different personas may come into play. The task responsibilities for the respective plans are outlined in more detail under each plans description section.

Onboarding Program Manager - The Onboarding Program Manager assumes some, or all, of the following responsibilities, depending on the needs of each account:
<ul>
	<li>Gather and consolidate the required customer environment information, and the specific needs of the customer to accurately enrol the HP DaaS devices.</li>
	<li>Develop and implement the on boarding project plan.</li>
	<li>Communicate progress to the customer, HP, and partner (if applicable) throughout the on boarding process.</li>
	<li>Complete the on boarding process promptly.</li>
	<li>Reduce deployment time while mitigating transition risks.</li>
	<li>Verify a successful implementation.</li>
	<li>Transition customer support for the HP DaaS Proactive Management capability to Service Experts.</li>
</ul>
HP Service Expert - The HP Service Experts primary responsibilities include:
<ul>
	<li>Create the HP DaaS Proactive Management account.</li>
	<li>Add or remove HP DaaS Proactive Management console users.</li>
	<li>Deploy MDM device policies and customer applications per customer request.</li>
	<li>Remove requested apps from the customers Device App Catalogue.</li>
	<li>Monitor device incidents in Proactive Management portal and notify customer when a device health issue is detected. Also, provide optimization and diagnostic tools to resolve health issues</li>
	<li>Provide requested reports.</li>
	<li>Troubleshoot installation and connectivity issues.</li>
	<li>Coordinate Windows update deployments and changes to Windows update installation policy in coordination with the customer.</li>
	<li>Assist customer and provide answers to service related questions.</li>
	<li>Help ensure compliance with HP DaaS Proactive Management subscription requirements.</li>
	<li>Attempt to remotely locate or erase data from a missing or stolen device.</li>
</ul>
Customer IT Device Administrator - The customers designated IT Administrator is responsible for the following tasks:
<ul>
	<li>Establish an HP DaaS account, working with their partner or HP account rep.</li>
	<li>Install the Proactive Management software onto their DaaS managed devices.</li>
	<li>Request to add or remove managed users and devices.</li>
	<li>Request application deployment or removal</li>
	<li>Test updates throughout the Windows 10 update life cycle, including application user acceptance with the updates. Also, communicate change requests with HP Service Expert team to enable them to adjust the updates rollout and associated ring settings.</li>
	<li>Review hardware, software, and other reports and respond as necessary.</li>
	<li>Troubleshoot and perform triage for common end-user support issues before escalating to HP support.</li>
	<li>Roll back OS updates in customer environment in case of a failure.</li>
	<li>Request device lock or data erase on a device reported missing or stolen.</li>
	<li>Ensure compliance with software application licensing requirements.</li>
	<li>Renew, change or cancel the HP DaaS account.</li>
</ul>
Note: Personnel authorized to access the Proactive Management console include a partner if the customer pre-approves a specific individual within the partner organization to have access to the customers Proactive Management account.

<strong>Other HP DaaS Proactive Management personas:</strong>

HP Account Delivery Manager (ADM):

HP Account Delivery Managers (ADM) may be included in some plans or can be added to an existing HP DaaS Proactive Management contract for an additional charge.

Customers who purchase HP DaaS Proactive Management through their preferred partner will sometimes designate their partner to have access to the HP DaaS Proactive Management portal and to serve as the primary point of contact for incident notifications in coordination with HP Service Experts.

The objective of an HP Account Delivery Manager (if applicable) is to help ensure HP is meeting its contract goals and be a proactive, trusted customer advisor. The ADMs primary responsibilities can include:
<ul>
	<li>Account transition and setup</li>
	<li>Business reviews</li>
	<li>Account planning</li>
	<li>Business Collaboration</li>
	<li>Contract administration</li>
	<li>Services and third-party management</li>
	<li>Socialize new Service features with the customer</li>
	<li>Internal HP deliverables</li>
	<li>Customer-specific requests</li>
</ul>
Partner:

The customers reseller or IT services partner, at the customers discretion, may take on some or all the customers responsibilities within the Proactive Management plan. In addition to that option, partners (if applicable) can be responsible for the following tasks:
<ul>
	<li>Ensure the HP Proactive Management Care Pack is registered.</li>
	<li>Schedule and host meetings with HP and customer as needed.</li>
	<li>If applicable, provide business insights and expert analysis for customer environment leveraging Proactive Management reports.</li>
	<li>If applicable, perform customer point of contact or other duties, if so designated by the end customer.</li>
	<li>Assist customer with device enrolment or troubleshooting as needed.</li>
	<li>Socialize new Service features with the customer</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

&nbsp;
<ol start="4">
	<li><strong>CUSTOMER ONBOARDING:</strong></li>
</ol>
Onboarding is the process of bringing all customer devices covered under the DaaS plan into the Proactive Management with HP TechPulse solution. This is critical for HP to deliver the service successfully. HP TechPulse can monitor and track the devices, collect data, and generate reports and actionable insights, once the customer has been successfully onboarded and all DaaS devices have been enrolled. This data collection is required for HP Service Experts to manage the customer devices in both the Enhanced and the Premium DaaS plans.

<strong>Onboarding Program Management:</strong>

An HP Onboarding Program Manager will be assigned to manage the onboarding process for the account if the customer purchases an HP DaaS Enhanced or Premium plan. Once the service is registered, the Onboarding Program Manager will manage the onboarding project from kick off to completion and is responsible for the successful onboarding of the account. Please refer to the Roles and Responsibilities section for more details about the scope of the Onboarding Program Manager role.

If the customer purchases the HP DaaS Standard plan, no dedicated Onboarding Program Manager will be assigned since it is a self-managed plan. Once a customer completes registration of the service, HP will review the information and create the account for the customer. HP Service Experts will also send a welcome email to the customer once account creation is complete. As a part of the welcome kit, customers will receive instructions on how to obtain assistance.

<strong>Onboarding process overview:</strong>

The onboarding process can be broken down into five phases:
<ul>
	<li>Phase 1 - Registration</li>
	<li>Phase 2 - Information gathering</li>
	<li>Phase 3 - HP Recommendations and Account Creation</li>
	<li>Phase 4  Deployment</li>
	<li>Phase 5  Transition to Ongoing Management</li>
</ul>
The registration process is the same for all plans, but it varies depending on how the service is purchased: through contract, Electronic Software Delivery SKUs, or Fixed Care Pack SKUs. The remaining phases vary depending on the plan purchased. If it is Premium or Enhanced plan, HP will have Onboarding Program Manager assigned, and lead through the onboarding process by working with customers. If the self-managed Standard plan is selected, HP will create the account, but the customer or partner will be responsible to complete the remaining tasks. HP will provide instructions to assist with these tasks.

The above phases will be explained in detail soon.

&nbsp;

<strong>To know more about HP DaaS Proactive Management , get in touch with us.</strong>

<strong>Call us on: +91 22 4031 6800</strong>
